<!DOCTYPE html><html lang="en" dir="ltr"> <head><meta charset="utf-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"/><base href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/"/><link rel="shortcut icon" href="favicon.svg" type="image/svg+xml"/><meta name="astro-view-transitions-enabled" content="true"><meta name="astro-view-transitions-fallback" content="animate"><script type="module" src="/docs/cesdk/_astro/ClientRouter.astro_astro_type_script_index_0_lang.CtSceO8m.js"></script><title>Disable or Enable Features - React | IMG.LY Docs</title><link rel="canonical" href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/react/user-interface/customization/disable-or-enable-f058e2/"><meta name="description" content="Control which editor features are available to users by enabling, disabling, or conditionally toggling them using the Feature API."><meta name="robots" content="index, follow"><meta property="og:title" content="Disable or Enable Features - React | IMG.LY Docs"><meta property="og:type" content="website"><meta property="og:image" content="https://img.ly//docs/cesdk/opengraph_docs.png"><meta property="og:url" content="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/react/user-interface/customization/disable-or-enable-f058e2/"><script>
      // Apply theme immediately to prevent flash
      (function () {
        function applyTheme() {
          const stored = localStorage.getItem('theme');
          const systemTheme = window.matchMedia?.(
            '(prefers-color-scheme: dark)',
          ).matches
            ? 'dark'
            : 'light';
          const theme = stored ?? systemTheme;

          // Always explicitly set the theme state
          if (theme === 'dark') {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
          } else {
            document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
          }
        }

        // Apply theme on initial load
        applyTheme();

        // Apply theme after Astro page swap (View Transitions)
        document.addEventListener('astro:after-swap', applyTheme);
      })();

  document.addEventListener('astro:before-preparation', event => {
    const originalLoader = event.loader;
    event.loader = async function () {
      const spinner = document.getElementById('page-transition-spinner');
      // If it takes more than 0.5s to load, show the spinner
      const h1 = document.getElementsByTagName('h1');
      const main = document.getElementsByTagName('main');
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
        spinner?.classList.remove('opacity-0');
        h1[0]?.classList.add('animate-pulse');
        main[0]?.classList.add('animate-pulse');
        spinner?.classList.remove('opacity-0');
      }, 500);
      await originalLoader();
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      spinner?.classList.add('opacity-0');
    };
  });
</script> <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://img.ly/static/imgly-website-components/imgly-website-components.css" as="style"><noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://img.ly/static/imgly-website-components/imgly-website-components.css"></noscript><div id="imgly-website-components-cookies"></div><script>

<p>The Feature API provides global control over feature visibility throughout the editor. Use it to hide delete buttons from certain users, disable crop controls based on context, or conditionally enable features based on user roles or selection state. Unlike the Component Order API which targets specific components in specific areas, the Feature API affects features everywhere in the editor at once.</p>

EditorPlugin, EditorPluginContext } from '@cesdk/cesdk-js';import {  BlurAssetSource,  ColorPaletteAssetSource,  CropPresetsAssetSource,  DemoAssetSources,  EffectsAssetSource,  FiltersAssetSource,  PagePresetsAssetSource,  StickerAssetSource,  TextAssetSource,  TextComponentAssetSource,  TypefaceAssetSource,  UploadAssetSources,  VectorShapeAssetSource} from '@cesdk/cesdk-js/plugins';import { DesignEditorConfig } from './design-editor/plugin';import packageJson from './package.json';/** * Disable or Enable Features Example * * This example demonstrates how to use CE.SDK's Feature API to: * - Enable and disable features with simple toggles * - Use glob patterns for bulk operations * - Create custom predicates based on selection * - Extend default predicates with additional conditions * - Check feature status and discover available features */class Example implements EditorPlugin {  name = packageJson.name;  version = packageJson.version;  async initialize({ cesdk }: EditorPluginContext): Promise<void> {    if (!cesdk) {      throw new Error('CE.SDK instance is required for this plugin');    }    await cesdk.addPlugin(new DesignEditorConfig());    // Add asset source plugins    await cesdk.addPlugin(new BlurAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new ColorPaletteAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new CropPresetsAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new UploadAssetSources({ include: ['ly.img.image.upload'] }));    await cesdk.addPlugin(      new DemoAssetSources({        include: [          'ly.img.templates.blank.*',          'ly.img.templates.presentation.*',          'ly.img.templates.print.*',          'ly.img.templates.social.*',          'ly.img.image.*'        ]      })    );    await cesdk.addPlugin(new EffectsAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new FiltersAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new PagePresetsAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new StickerAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new TextAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new TextComponentAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new TypefaceAssetSource());    await cesdk.addPlugin(new VectorShapeAssetSource());    await cesdk.actions.run('scene.create', {      page: {        sourceId: 'ly.img.page.presets',        assetId: 'ly.img.page.presets.print.iso.a6.landscape'      }    });    const engine = cesdk.engine;    // Enable delete feature with default predicate    cesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.delete');    // Enable multiple features at once    cesdk.feature.enable(['ly.img.duplicate', 'ly.img.group']);    // Disable crop feature    cesdk.feature.disable('ly.img.crop');    // Disable multiple features at once    cesdk.feature.disable(['ly.img.notifications', 'ly.img.preview']);    // Disable all transform features using glob pattern    cesdk.feature.disable('ly.img.transform*');    // Enable all video features using glob pattern    cesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.video*');    // Set feature with boolean (terminal predicate)    cesdk.feature.set('ly.img.fill', true);    // Set feature with custom predicate based on selection    cesdk.feature.set('ly.img.duplicate', ({ engine }) => {      return engine.block.findAllSelected().length > 0;    });    // Extend default predicate with additional condition    cesdk.feature.set('ly.img.delete', ({ defaultPredicate }) => {      // Only allow delete in design mode      return defaultPredicate() &#38;&#38; engine.scene.getMode() === 'Design';    });    // Chain multiple predicates using isPreviousEnable    cesdk.feature.set('ly.img.replace', ({ isPreviousEnable, engine }) => {      const previousResult = isPreviousEnable();      const hasSelection = engine.block.findAllSelected().length > 0;      return previousResult &#38;&#38; hasSelection;    });    // Check if a feature is enabled    const isDeleteEnabled = cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.delete');    console.log('Delete feature enabled:', isDeleteEnabled);    // Check if all video features are enabled (returns true only if ALL match)    const allVideoEnabled = cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.video*');    console.log('All video features enabled:', allVideoEnabled);    // List all registered feature IDs    const allFeatures = cesdk.feature.list();    console.log('All features:', allFeatures.slice(0, 10), '...');    // List features matching a pattern    const navigationFeatures = cesdk.feature.list({      matcher: 'ly.img.navigation*'    });    console.log('Navigation features:', navigationFeatures);    cesdk.ui.insertOrderComponent(      { in: 'ly.img.navigation.bar', position: 'end' },      {        id: 'ly.img.actions.navigationBar',        children: [          {            id: 'ly.img.action.navigationBar',            key: 'toggle-dock',            label: 'Toggle Dock',            onClick: () => {              const enabled = cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.dock');              if (enabled) {                cesdk.feature.disable('ly.img.dock');                console.log('Dock feature disabled');              } else {                cesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.dock');                console.log('Dock feature enabled');              } console.log('All crop features disabled');              } else {                cesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.crop*');                console.log('All crop features enabled');              }            }          },          {            id: 'ly.img.action.navigationBar',            key: 'log-status',            label: 'Log Feature Status',            icon: '@imgly/Info', 'Duplicate:',                cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.duplicate')              );              console.log('Crop:', cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.crop'));              console.log('Fill:', cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.fill'));              console.log(                'Navigation features:',                cesdk.feature.list({ matcher: 'ly.img.navigation*' })              );            }          }        ]      }    );    const page = engine.block.findByType('page')[0];    const pageWidth = engine.block.getWidth(page);    const pageHeight = engine.block.getHeight(page);    const gradientFill = engine.block.createFill('gradient/linear');    engine.block.setFill(page, gradientFill);    engine.block.setGradientColorStops(gradientFill, 'fill/gradient/colors', [      { color: { r: 0.99, g: 0.98, b: 0.97, a: 1 }, stop: 0 },      { color: { r: 0.97, g: 0.96, b: 0.94, a: 1 }, stop: 1 }    ]);    engine.block.setFloat(gradientFill, 'fill/gradient/linear/startPointX', 0);    engine.block.setFloat(gradientFill, 'fill/gradient/linear/startPointY', 0);    engine.block.setFloat(gradientFill, 'fill/gradient/linear/endPointX', 1);    engine.block.setFloat(gradientFill, 'fill/gradient/linear/endPointY', 1);    const titleBlock = engine.block.create('text');    engine.block.appendChild(page, titleBlock); engine.block.setSelected(titleBlock, true);    console.log('Disable or Enable Features example loaded successfully!');  }}export default Example;"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>This guide covers how to enable and disable features with simple toggles, create custom predicates for conditional feature access, use glob patterns for bulk operations, and debug feature configurations.</p>
<h2 id="feature-api-methods">Feature API Methods<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#feature-api-methods">#</a></h2>
<p>The following table summarizes the main Feature API methods and when to use each:</p>

































<table><thead><tr><th>Method</th><th>Use Case</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.enable()</code></td><td>Enable features with their default predicates</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.disable()</code></td><td>Disable features (hide from UI)</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.set()</code></td><td>Set features with custom predicates or boolean values</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.isEnabled()</code></td><td>Check if a feature is currently enabled</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.list()</code></td><td>Discover registered feature IDs</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.get()</code></td><td>Get predicate chain for debugging</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2 id="enable-features">Enable Features<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#enable-features">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>cesdk.feature.enable()</code> to activate a feature with its default predicate behavior. The method accepts a single feature ID, an array of IDs, or a glob pattern.</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Enable delete feature with default predicate</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">enable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.delete&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Enable delete feature with default predicatecesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.delete');"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>You can enable multiple features at once by passing an array:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Enable multiple features at once</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">enable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">([</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.duplicate&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.group&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">]);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Enable multiple features at oncecesdk.feature.enable(['ly.img.duplicate', 'ly.img.group']);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>Glob patterns allow you to enable all features matching a pattern. The <code>*</code> wildcard matches any sequence of characters:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Enable all video features using glob pattern</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">enable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.video*&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Enable all video features using glob patterncesdk.feature.enable('ly.img.video*');"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<h2 id="disable-features">Disable Features<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#disable-features">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>cesdk.feature.disable()</code> to hide features from the UI. Like <code>enable()</code>, it accepts single IDs, arrays, or glob patterns.</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Disable crop feature</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">disable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.crop&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Disable crop featurecesdk.feature.disable('ly.img.crop');"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>Disable multiple features at once by passing an array:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Disable multiple features at once</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">disable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">([</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.notifications&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.preview&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">]);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Disable multiple features at oncecesdk.feature.disable(['ly.img.notifications', 'ly.img.preview']);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>Use glob patterns to disable all features matching a pattern:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Disable all transform features using glob pattern</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">disable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.transform*&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Disable all transform features using glob patterncesdk.feature.disable('ly.img.transform*');"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<h2 id="custom-predicates">Custom Predicates<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#custom-predicates">#</a></h2>
<p>The <code>cesdk.feature.set()</code> method allows you to configure features with custom logic. You can pass a boolean value or a function predicate.</p>
<h3 id="boolean-predicates">Boolean Predicates<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#boolean-predicates">#</a></h3>
<p>Passing <code>true</code> or <code>false</code> creates a terminal predicate that overrides any <code>enable()</code> or <code>disable()</code> calls:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Set feature with boolean (terminal predicate)</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">set</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.fill&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">true</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Set feature with boolean (terminal predicate)cesdk.feature.set('ly.img.fill', true);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<aside class="prose-p:m-0 prose-h2:m-0 prose-h3:m-0 mb-8 rounded-lg border px-6 py-4 text-sm bg-imglygray-200 dark:bg-imglygray-900 border-imglygray-600 dark:border-dark-imglygray-300 dark:text-imglygray-300 text-imglygray-900 border-imglygray-600 "> <p>Boolean predicates are terminal. Once you use <code>set()</code> with a boolean, subsequent <code>enable()</code> or <code>disable()</code> calls won’t affect that feature because the boolean predicate evaluates first.</p> </aside>
<h3 id="function-predicates">Function Predicates<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#function-predicates">#</a></h3>
<p>Function predicates receive a context object with <code>engine</code>, <code>isPreviousEnable()</code>, and <code>defaultPredicate()</code>. Use them for dynamic conditions based on selection or other state:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Set feature with custom predicate based on selection</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">set</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.duplicate&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, ({ </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> }) </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">return</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">block</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">findAllSelected</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">().</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">length</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#08774E;--1:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Set feature with custom predicate based on selectioncesdk.feature.set('ly.img.duplicate', ({ engine }) => {  return engine.block.findAllSelected().length > 0;});"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>This predicate enables the duplicate feature only when at least one block is selected.</p>
<h3 id="extending-default-behavior">Extending Default Behavior<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#extending-default-behavior">#</a></h3>
<p>You can build on a feature’s default predicate using <code>defaultPredicate()</code>. This lets you add conditions while preserving the built-in logic:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Extend default predicate with additional condition</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">set</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.delete&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, ({ </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">defaultPredicate</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> }) </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Only allow delete in design mode</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">return</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">defaultPredicate</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">() </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&amp;&amp;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">scene</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">getMode</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">() </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">===</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;Design&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Extend default predicate with additional conditioncesdk.feature.set('ly.img.delete', ({ defaultPredicate }) => {  // Only allow delete in design mode  return defaultPredicate() &#38;&#38; engine.scene.getMode() === 'Design';});"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<h3 id="layering-conditions">Layering Conditions<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#layering-conditions">#</a></h3>
<p>Use <code>isPreviousEnable()</code> to chain with previously registered predicates. This enables layered conditions from multiple <code>set()</code> calls:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Chain multiple predicates using isPreviousEnable</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">set</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.replace&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, ({ </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">isPreviousEnable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> }) </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">previousResult</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">isPreviousEnable</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">();</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">hasSelection</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">block</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">findAllSelected</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">().</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">length</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#08774E;--1:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">return</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">previousResult</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&amp;&amp;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">hasSelection</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Chain multiple predicates using isPreviousEnablecesdk.feature.set('ly.img.replace', ({ isPreviousEnable, engine }) => {  const previousResult = isPreviousEnable();  const hasSelection = engine.block.findAllSelected().length > 0;  return previousResult &#38;&#38; hasSelection;});"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<h2 id="evaluation-order">Evaluation Order<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#evaluation-order">#</a></h2>
<p>When multiple predicates are registered for a feature, they evaluate in this order:</p>
<ol>
<li>Most recent <code>set()</code> predicates run first</li>
<li>Older <code>set()</code> predicates in reverse chronological order</li>
<li><code>enable()</code>/<code>disable()</code> state runs last</li>
</ol>
<p>Boolean predicates are terminal and immediately return their value without continuing the chain. Function predicates control whether to continue by calling <code>isPreviousEnable()</code> or returning directly.</p>
<h2 id="glob-patterns">Glob Patterns<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#glob-patterns">#</a></h2>
<p>All main Feature API methods support glob pattern matching for bulk operations. The <code>*</code> wildcard matches any sequence of characters within a segment.</p>
<p>Supported methods:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>cesdk.feature.enable(&#39;ly.img.video.*&#39;)</code> - Enable all video features</li>
<li><code>cesdk.feature.disable(&#39;ly.img.crop.*&#39;)</code> - Disable all crop features</li>
<li><code>cesdk.feature.set(&#39;ly.img.navigation.*&#39;, predicate)</code> - Set all navigation features</li>
<li><code>cesdk.feature.isEnabled(&#39;ly.img.video.*&#39;)</code> - Check if ALL matching features are enabled</li>
<li><code>cesdk.feature.list({ matcher: &#39;ly.img.video.*&#39; })</code> - List matching features</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="check-feature-status">Check Feature Status<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#check-feature-status">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>cesdk.feature.isEnabled()</code> to query if a feature is currently enabled:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Check if a feature is enabled</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">isDeleteEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">isEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.delete&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">console</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">log</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;Delete feature enabled:&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">isDeleteEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Check if a feature is enabledconst isDeleteEnabled = cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.delete');console.log('Delete feature enabled:', isDeleteEnabled);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>When using a glob pattern with <code>isEnabled()</code>, it returns <code>true</code> only if all matching features are enabled:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#007A00;--1:#7AA468">// Check if all video features are enabled (returns true only if ALL match)</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">allVideoEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">isEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;ly.img.video*&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">console</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">log</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;All video features enabled:&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">allVideoEnabled</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="// Check if all video features are enabled (returns true only if ALL match)const allVideoEnabled = cesdk.feature.isEnabled('ly.img.video*');console.log('All video features enabled:', allVideoEnabled);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<h2 id="discover-features">Discover Features<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#discover-features">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>cesdk.feature.list()</code> to get all registered feature IDs. You can filter with the optional <code>matcher</code> parameter:</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">feature</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;All features:&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">allFeatures</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">slice</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#08774E;--1:#B5CEA8">0</span><span <h2 id="troubleshooting">Troubleshooting<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#troubleshooting">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="feature-not-visible">Feature Not Visible<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#feature-not-visible">#</a></h3>
<p>If a feature doesn’t appear in the UI after calling <code>enable()</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li>Check if a <code>set()</code> call with a boolean is overriding it. Boolean predicates are terminal and take precedence.</li>
<li>Verify the feature ID spelling matches exactly.</li>
<li>Confirm the feature is relevant for the current context (e.g., video features only appear in Video mode).</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="disable-not-working"><code>disable()</code> Not Working<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#disable-not-working">#</a></h3>
<p>If <code>disable()</code> doesn’t hide a feature:</p>
<ol>
<li>Check if a <code>set()</code> predicate exists for that feature. The <code>set()</code> predicates evaluate before <code>disable()</code>.</li>
<li>Use <code>cesdk.feature.get()</code> to inspect the predicate chain.</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="glob-pattern-not-matching">Glob Pattern Not Matching<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#glob-pattern-not-matching">#</a></h3>
<p>If a glob pattern doesn’t affect expected features:</p>
<ol>
<li>Verify the pattern syntax is correct.</li>
<li>Use <code>cesdk.feature.list({ matcher: &#39;your.pattern.*&#39; })</code> to see which features match.</li>
<li>Check that features are registered before applying the pattern.</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="api-reference">API Reference<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#api-reference">#</a></h2>








































<table><thead><tr><th>Method</th><th>Signature</th><th>Purpose</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.enable()</code></td><td><code>enable(featureId: FeatureId | FeatureId[]): void</code></td><td>Enable features with default predicates</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.disable()</code></td><td><code>disable(featureId: FeatureId | FeatureId[]): void</code></td><td>Disable features</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.set()</code></td><td><code>set(featureId: FeatureId, enabled: boolean | FeaturePredicate): void</code></td><td>Set feature state with custom predicates</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.isEnabled()</code></td><td><code>isEnabled(featureId: FeatureId, context?: FeatureContext): boolean</code></td><td>Check if feature is enabled</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.list()</code></td><td><code>list(options?: { matcher?: string }): FeatureId[]</code></td><td>List registered feature IDs</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.feature.get()</code></td><td><code>get(featureId: FeatureId): FeaturePredicate[] | undefined</code></td><td>Get predicate chain for debugging</td></tr></tbody></table>
